Let's Logic Collection ID: 600
Title: Mass Remodel
Author: Various Authors
Description: A mass collection of remodels, made by various authors. Each level has the original author and the remodelist(s) stated. The collection has also been scaned for duplicates.

It is Not allowed to make this collection a part of any payable Sokoban program, such as Bjorn Kallmark's sokoban etc. You can make it a part of any freeware programs though.
